 in) aapako bataa den ki railway recruitment board group di (RRB Group D) ke 62 hajaar 907 padon par bhartee pariksha kara rahaa he
 The admit cards for the exam (RRB Admit Card) are being issued 4 days before the exam
 pariksha 17 disambar tak chalane vaali he
 Candidates who have passed the first stage of Group d examination will get the physical efficiency test of the second stage

 Time-wise details of events related to the announcement of the formation of separate Telangana state from Andhra Pradesh: 1948: Indian Army annexed the princely state of Hyderabad including Telangana to India
 1 november 1956:madras state se telugana ko alag kar andhra state main shaamil kar telugubhashiyon ke liye ek alag rajya andhra pradesh kii sthapana kii gai
 1969: Start of 'jai Telangana' movement to declare Telangana a separate state
 police kii golibari main 300 se adhik logon kii maut
 1972: Start of 'jai Andhra' movement in coastal areas of Andhra Pradesh
 1997:bhartiya janata party (bhaajapa) telugana ke samarthan main ai, tathaa 1998 ke chunaav main usne 'ek mat, do rajya' ke naare ke saath chunaav ladaa

 to keep the Telangana agitation alive

 2004: TRS contested jointly with Congress and won five Lok Sabha seats and 26 assembly seats

 es
